[0:07:57] Crosseye_Jack: @AinzN Sorry was poking at things. Yeah my K95 RGB started to fail. Thing is, the keyboard is pretty standard layout, so I basically found a layout editor online, Tweaked a UK board to match the layout of the K95, then routed LEDs, then shipped that off to JLCPCB to make the board. In the end it cost me about the same a new board would of cost (Keyboard manifactures benefit for ordering in bluk). But it was fun to do. :-) There is a pretty decent open source keyboard community out there
